    40	const (
    41	        // keep the enqueue period a smaller value to make sure the BSL can be validated as expected.
    42	        // The BSL validation frequency is 1 minute by default, if we set the enqueue period as 1 minute,
    43	        // this will cause the actual validation interval for each BSL to be 2 minutes
    44	        bslValidationEnqueuePeriod = 10 * time.Second
    45	)
    46	
    47	// BackupStorageLocationReconciler reconciles a BackupStorageLocation object
    48	type backupStorageLocationReconciler struct {
    49	        ctx                       context.Context
    50	        client                    client.Client
    51	        defaultBackupLocationInfo storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo
    52	        // use variables to refer to these functions so they can be
    53	        // replaced with fakes for testing.
    54	        newPluginManager  func(logrus.FieldLogger) clientmgmt.Manager
    55	        backupStoreGetter persistence.ObjectBackupStoreGetter
    56	
    57	        log logrus.FieldLogger
    58	}
    59	
    60	// NewBackupStorageLocationReconciler initialize and return a backupStorageLocationReconciler struct
    61	func NewBackupStorageLocationReconciler(
    62	        ctx context.Context,
    63	        client client.Client,
    64	        defaultBackupLocationInfo storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo,
    65	        newPluginManager func(logrus.FieldLogger) clientmgmt.Manager,
    66	        backupStoreGetter persistence.ObjectBackupStoreGetter,
    67	        log logrus.FieldLogger) *backupStorageLocationReconciler {
    68	        return &backupStorageLocationReconciler{
    69	                ctx:                       ctx,
    70	                client:                    client,
    71	                defaultBackupLocationInfo: defaultBackupLocationInfo,
    72	                newPluginManager:          newPluginManager,
    73	                backupStoreGetter:         backupStoreGetter,
    74	                log:                       log,
    75	        }
    76	}
    77	
    78	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=velero.io,resources=backupstoragelocations,verbs=get;list;watch;create;update;patch;delete
    79	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=velero.io,resources=backupstoragelocations/status,verbs=get;update;patch
    80	
    81	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
    82	        var unavailableErrors []string
    83	        var location velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
    84	
    85	        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).WithField(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation, req.NamespacedName.String())
    86	        log.Debug("Validating availability of BackupStorageLocation")
    87	
    88	        locationList, err := storage.ListBackupStorageLocations(r.ctx, r.client, req.Namespace)
    89	        if err != nil {
    90	                log.WithError(err).Error("No BackupStorageLocations found, at least one is required")
    91	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        pluginManager := r.newPluginManager(log)
    95	        defer pluginManager.CleanupClients()
    96	
    97	        // find the BSL that matches the request
    98	        for _, bsl := range locationList.Items {
    99	                if bsl.Name == req.Name && bsl.Namespace == req.Namespace {
   100	                        location = bsl
   101	                }
   102	        }
   103	
   104	        if location.Name == "" || location.Namespace == "" {
   105	                log.WithError(err).Error("BackupStorageLocation is not found")
   106	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        // decide the default BSL
   110	        defaultFound, err := r.ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList)
   111	        if err != nil {
   112	                log.WithError(err).Error("failed to ensure single default bsl")
   113	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        func() {
   117	                var err error
   118	                original := location.DeepCopy()
   119	                defer func() {
   120	                        location.Status.LastValidationTime = &metav1.Time{Time: time.Now().UTC()}
   121	                        if err != nil {
   122	                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocation is invalid, marking as unavailable")
   123	                                err = errors.Wrapf(err, "BackupStorageLocation %q is unavailable", location.Name)
   124	                                unavailableErrors = append(unavailableErrors, err.Error())
   125	                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable
   126	                                location.Status.Message = err.Error()
   127	                        } else {
   128	                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocations is valid, marking as available")
   129	                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable
   130	                                location.Status.Message = ""
   131	                        }
   132	                        if err := r.client.Patch(r.ctx, &location, client.MergeFrom(original)); err != nil {
   133	                                log.WithError(err).Error("Error updating BackupStorageLocation phase")
   134	                        }
   135	                }()
   136	
   137	                backupStore, err := r.backupStoreGetter.Get(&location, pluginManager, log)
   138	                if err != nil {
   139	                        log.WithError(err).Error("Error getting a backup store")
   140	                        return
   141	                }
   142	
   143	                log.Info("Validating BackupStorageLocation")
   144	                err = backupStore.IsValid()
   145	                if err != nil {
   146	                        log.WithError(err).Error("fail to validate backup store")
   147	                        return
   148	                }
   149	        }()
   150	
   151	        r.logReconciledPhase(defaultFound, locationList, unavailableErrors)
   152	
   153	        return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   154	}
   155	
   156	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) logReconciledPhase(defaultFound bool, locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList, errs []string) {
   157	        var availableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   158	        var unAvailableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   159	        var unknownBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   160	        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation)
   161	
   162	        for i, location := range locationList.Items {
   163	                phase := location.Status.Phase
   164	                switch phase {
   165	                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable:
   166	                        availableBSLs = append(availableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   167	                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable:
   168	                        unAvailableBSLs = append(unAvailableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   169	                default:
   170	                        unknownBSLs = append(unknownBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   171	                }
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        numAvailable := len(availableBSLs)
   175	        numUnavailable := len(unAvailableBSLs)
   176	        numUnknown := len(unknownBSLs)
   177	
   178	        if numUnavailable+numUnknown == len(locationList.Items) { // no available BSL
   179	                if len(errs) > 0 {
   180	                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
   181	                } else {
   182	                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown)
   183	                }
   184	        } else if numUnavailable > 0 { // some but not all BSL unavailable
   185	                log.Warnf("Unavailable BackupStorageLocations detected: available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        if !defaultFound {
   189	                log.Warn("There is no existing BackupStorageLocation set as default. Please see `velero backup-location -h` for options.")
   190	        }
   191	}
   192	
   193	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
   194	        gp := kube.NewGenericEventPredicate(func(object client.Object) bool {
   195	                location := object.(*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation)
   196	                return storage.IsReadyToValidate(location.Spec.ValidationFrequency, location.Status.LastValidationTime, r.defaultBackupLocationInfo.ServerValidationFrequency, r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation))
   197	        })
   198	        g := kube.NewPeriodicalEnqueueSource(
   199	                r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation),
   200	                mgr.GetClient(),
   201	                &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList{},
   202	                bslValidationEnqueuePeriod,
   203	                kube.PeriodicalEnqueueSourceOption{
   204	                        Predicates: []predicate.Predicate{gp},
   205	                },
   206	        )
   207	
   208	        return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
   209	                // As the "status.LastValidationTime" field is always updated, this triggers new reconciling process, skip the update event that include no spec change to avoid the reconcile loop
   210	                For(&velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}, builder.WithPredicates(kube.SpecChangePredicate{})).
   211	                WatchesRawSource(g).
   212	                Named(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).
   213	                Complete(r)
   214	}
   215	
   216	// ensureSingleDefaultBSL ensures that there is only one default BSL in the namespace.
   217	// the default BSL priority is as follows:
   218	// 1. follow the user's setting (the most recent validation BSL is the default BSL)
   219	// 2. follow the server's setting ("velero server --default-backup-storage-location")
   220	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList) (bool, error) {

// RegisterBackupStorageLocationLastStatus records the last status of the backup storage location.

func (m *ServerMetrics) RegisterCSISnapshotSuccesses(backupSchedule, backupName string, csiSnapshotCompleted int) {
	if c, ok := m.metrics[csiSnapshotSuccessTotal].(*prometheus.CounterVec); ok {

// RegisterCSISnapshotFailures records a failed volume snapshot by CSI plugin.
func (m *ServerMetrics) RegisterCSISnapshotFailures(backupSchedule, backupName string, csiSnapshotsFailed int) {
	if c, ok := m.metrics[csiSnapshotFailureTotal].(*prometheus.CounterVec); ok {
		c.WithLabelValues(backupSchedule, backupName).Add(float64(csiSnapshotsFailed))
	}
}

// RegisterBackupStorageLocationLastStatus records the last status of the backup storage location.

g.WithLabelValues(bslName).Set(float64(lastStatus))
}
